<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" ALIGN="center">

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Walgreens Boots Alliance Reports Fiscal 2020 Second Quarter Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Business Performance on Track; Quarter Ahead of Company&#146;s Expectations </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Second quarter highlights, year-over-year </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Sales increased 3.7&nbsp;percent to $35.8&nbsp;billion, up 4.1&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Operating income decreased 18.7&nbsp;percent to $1.2&nbsp;billion; Adjusted operating income decreased
12.0&nbsp;percent to $1.7&nbsp;billion, on both a reported and constant currency basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">EPS decreased 14.0&nbsp;percent to $1.07; Adjusted EPS decreased 7.3&nbsp;percent to $1.52, on both a reported
and constant currency basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Year-to-date</FONT></FONT> highlights
</I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Net cash provided by operating activities in the first half of fiscal 2020 was $2.5&nbsp;billion, an increase of
$1.3&nbsp;billion compared with the same period a year ago; Free cash flow was $1.8&nbsp;billion, an increase of $1.4&nbsp;billion </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Fiscal 2020 outlook </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Prior to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> pandemic, the company was on track to maintain
fiscal 2020 guidance of roughly flat growth in adjusted EPS, at constant currency rates, plus or minus 3&nbsp;percent </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Future impacts of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> uncertain; updates will be provided in the
next earnings report </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Transformational Cost Management Program </I></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Company on target to deliver in excess of $1.8&nbsp;billion in annual cost savings by fiscal 2022
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">DEERFIELD, Ill., April&nbsp;2, 2020&#151;Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (Nasdaq:&nbsp;WBA) today announced financial results for the
second quarter of fiscal 2020, which ended February&nbsp;29, 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Executive Vice Chairman and CEO Stefano Pessina said, &#147;We are pleased to report
second quarter results exceeding our expectations, with sequential improvement in comparable U.S. prescription volume and retail sales. During these unprecedented times of global uncertainty, Walgreens Boots Alliance is on the front lines of
combating the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> pandemic. Our number one priority is to continue to provide essential services, products and information at this critical moment of need, demonstrating our unwavering commitment to our
customers and patients, and to our people.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Overview of Second Quarter Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fiscal 2020 second quarter net earnings attributable to WBA decreased 18.2&nbsp;percent to $946&nbsp;million compared with the same quarter a year ago, while
net earnings per share<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> decreased 14.0&nbsp;percent to $1.07 compared with the same quarter a year ago. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted net earnings attributable to WBA<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> decreased 11.8&nbsp;percent to $1.3&nbsp;billion, on both a
reported and constant currency basis, compared with the same quarter a year ago. Adjusted earnings per share were $1.52, a decrease of 7.3&nbsp;percent on both a reported and constant currency basis, compared with the same quarter a year ago. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales in the second quarter were $35.8&nbsp;billion, an increase of 3.7&nbsp;percent from the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, and an increase of 4.1&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. Effects from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> pandemic began at the end of the second quarter and were not
material to overall results. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Compared to the same quarter a year ago, operating income was $1.2&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 18.7&nbsp;percent, and
adjusted operating income was $1.7&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 12.0&nbsp;percent, on both a reported and constant currency basis, reflecting lower U.S. pharmacy gross margin and year-over-year bonus changes, partially offset by cost savings from the
Transformational Cost Management Program. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net cash provided by operating activities was $1.4&nbsp;billion in the second quarter and free cash flow was
$1.1&nbsp;billion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Overview of Fiscal 2020 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Year-to-Date</FONT></FONT> Results
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the first six months of fiscal 2020, net earnings attributable to WBA decreased 21.4&nbsp;percent to $1.8&nbsp;billion compared with the same
period a year ago, while net earnings per share<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1 </SUP>decreased 16.8&nbsp;percent to $2.01 compared with the same period a year ago. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted net earnings attributable to WBA<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> for the first six months of fiscal 2020, decreased
11.8&nbsp;percent to $2.6&nbsp;billion, down 11.7&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, compared with the same period a year ago. Adjusted earnings per share for the first six months of fiscal 2020 were $2.88, a decrease of 6.6&nbsp;percent on
a reported basis and a decrease of 6.5&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, compared with the same period a year ago. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales in the first six months
of fiscal 2020 were $70.2&nbsp;billion, an increase of 2.7&nbsp;percent from the same period a year ago, and an increase of 3.2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income in the first six months of fiscal 2020 was $2.2&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 23.0&nbsp;percent from the same period a year ago. Adjusted
operating income in the first six months of the fiscal year was $3.2&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 13.7&nbsp;percent from the same period a year ago, and a decrease of 13.6&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net cash provided by operating activities was $2.5&nbsp;billion in the first six months of fiscal 2020, an increase of $1.3&nbsp;billion from the same period
last year, and free cash flow was $1.8&nbsp;billion, an increase of $1.4&nbsp;billion from the same period a year ago, reflecting strong working capital performance, prior year headwinds and favorable timing. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Company Outlook </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Prior to the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> pandemic, the company was on track to maintain its guidance for full-year fiscal 2020, of roughly flat growth in adjusted EPS, at constant currency rates, with a range of plus or minus 3&nbsp;percent.
Second quarter financial performance exceeded the company&#146;s expectations. Although the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> situation is ultimately temporary, given the many rapidly changing variables related to the pandemic, at
this time WBA is not in a position to accurately forecast the future impacts. The company will continue to closely assess and manage this situation, and will provide further updates in the next earnings report when both the potential positive and
negative effects of the pandemic will be known in more detail. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Progress on Strategic Priorities </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the second quarter of fiscal 2020, and since the close of the quarter, the company made substantial progress on its four strategic priorities:
accelerating digitalization; transforming and restructuring its retail offering; creating neighborhood health destinations; and the Transformational Cost Management Program. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA has taken numerous steps to support customers, patients and team members during the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> pandemic. The

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Expanded temporary benefits for certain team members </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Business Divisions </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Retail Pharmacy USA: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Retail Pharmacy USA had second quarter sales of $27.2&nbsp;billion, an increase of 3.8&nbsp;percent over the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
quarter. Sales in comparable stores increased 2.7&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Comparable data in this press release exclude the favorable impact of the 2020 leap day. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Pharmacy sales increased 5.3&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting higher brand inflation and
prescription volume, and specialty growth of 17.7&nbsp;percent. Comparable pharmacy sales increased 3.7&nbsp;percent. The division filled 296.8&nbsp;million prescriptions, including immunizations, adjusted to
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalents in the quarter, an increase of 3.7&nbsp;percent over the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Prescriptions filled in comparable stores increased 4.9&nbsp;percent
compared with the same quarter a year ago. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The division&#146;s retail prescription market share on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT>
adjusted basis in the second quarter decreased approximately 50 basis points over the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to 21.0&nbsp;percent, as reported by IQVIA.<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Retail sales decreased 0.3&nbsp;percent in the second quarter compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period. Comparable retail
sales were up 0.6&nbsp;percent in the quarter, mostly due to strong growth in health and wellness, including a favorable cough, cold and flu season. Excluding tobacco and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-cigarettes,</FONT> comparable retail sales
increased 1.9&nbsp;percent. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross profit decreased 4.3&nbsp;percent compared with the same quarter a year ago and adjusted gross profit decreased
3.7&nbsp;percent, with procurement savings, prescription growth and solid retail growth more than offset by reimbursement pressure. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Second quarter
selling, general and administrative expenses&nbsp;(SG&amp;A) as a percentage of sales decreased by 0.7 percentage point compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted SG&amp;A as a percentage of sales decreased
by 0.8 percentage point. Both decreases include savings from the Transformational Cost Management Program. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income in the second quarter
decreased 21.5&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $963&nbsp;million. Excluding costs related to the acquisition of Rite Aid stores and to the Transformational Cost Management Program, adjusted operating
income in the second quarter decreased 12.9&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $1.3&nbsp;billion, reflecting the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-on-year</FONT></FONT> bonus impact and a reimbursement contract <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">true-up.</FONT> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Retail Pharmacy International: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Retail Pharmacy
International had second quarter sales of $3.1&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 0.8&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, including a favorable currency impact of 0.9&nbsp;percent. Sales decreased
1.7&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, mainly due to a 1.2&nbsp;percent decline in Boots&nbsp;UK sales and lower sales in Thailand and Chile. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Comparable pharmacy sales in Boots&nbsp;UK increased 1.8&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis,
reflecting higher National Health Service&nbsp;(NHS) reimbursement, partially offset by lower prescription volume. Boots UK comparable retail sales decreased 4.6&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. Overall, the business held share in its
categories, in a declining market. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross profit increased 0.3&nbsp;percent compared with the same quarter a year ago, including a favorable currency
impact of 0.8&nbsp;percent. Adjusted gross profit decreased 2.5&nbsp;percent, on a constant currency basis, reflecting lower retail sales and margin in Boots UK. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">SG&amp;A as a percentage of sales increased 2.3 percentage points, including incremental costs associated with the Transformational Cost Management Program.
Adjusted SG&amp;A as a percentage of sales, on a constant currency basis, increased 1.6 percentage points. Both reflected the higher <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-on-year</FONT></FONT> bonus impact and higher
technology investments. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income in the second quarter decreased 31.4&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
quarter to $132&nbsp;million, while adjusted operating income decreased 22.9&nbsp;percent to $198&nbsp;million, down 24.0&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Pharmaceutical Wholesale: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Pharmaceutical Wholesale had
second quarter sales of $6.1&nbsp;billion, an increase of 5.7&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, including an adverse currency impact of 2.3&nbsp;percent. On a constant currency basis, sales increased
8.0&nbsp;percent, led by emerging markets and the&nbsp;UK. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income in the second quarter was $136&nbsp;million, which included $28&nbsp;million
from the company&#146;s equity earnings in AmerisourceBergen. This compared with operating income of $100&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, which included $83&nbsp;million from the company&#146;s equity
earnings in AmerisourceBergen. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted operating income increased 4.6&nbsp;percent to $235&nbsp;million, up 5.2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency
basis, reflecting strong sales growth and a higher contribution from AmerisourceBergen, partially offset by lower gross margin. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Dividends Declared
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the second quarter, the company declared a quarterly dividend of 45.75 cents per share, unchanged from the previous quarter and an increase of
4&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. The dividend was payable March&nbsp;12, 2020 to stockholders of record as of February&nbsp;19, 2020. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Conference Call </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA will hold a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-hour</FONT> conference call to discuss the second quarter results beginning at 8:30 a.m. Eastern time today, April&nbsp;2, 2020. The conference call will be simulcast through the WBA investor relations website at:
<U>http://investor.walgreensbootsalliance.com</U>. A replay of the conference call will be archived on the website for 12 months after the&nbsp;call. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
replay also will be available from 11:30&nbsp;a.m. Eastern time, April&nbsp;2 through April&nbsp;9, 2020, by calling +1&nbsp;800&nbsp;585&nbsp;8367 within the&nbsp;U.S. and Canada, or +1&nbsp;416&nbsp;621&nbsp;4642 outside the U.S. and Canada, using
replay code 4048187. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="line-height:8.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000;width:11%">&nbsp;</P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>We do not undertake, and expressly disclaim, any duty or obligation to update publicly any

used in this release to the most comparable GAAP financial measure and related disclosures. </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">ENDS </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Notes to Editors: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Walgreens Boots Alliance
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Walgreens Boots Alliance (Nasdaq:&nbsp;WBA) is a global leader in retail and wholesale pharmacy, touching millions of lives every day through
dispensing and distributing medicines, its convenient retail locations, digital platforms and health and beauty products. The company has more than 100 years of trusted health care heritage and innovation in community pharmacy and pharmaceutical
wholesaling. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Including equity method investments, WBA has a presence in more than 25 countries, employs more than 440,000 people and has more than 18,750
stores. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA&#146;s purpose is to help people across the world lead healthier and happier lives. The company is proud of its contributions to healthy
communities, a healthy planet, an inclusive workplace and a sustainable marketplace. The company&#146;s businesses have been recognized for their Corporate Social Responsibility. Walgreens was named to FORTUNE* magazine&#146;s 2019 Companies that
Change the World list and Boots UK was recognized as Responsible Business of the Year 2019-2020 by Business in the Community. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA is included in
FORTUNE&#146;s 2020 list of the World&#146;s Most Admired Companies. This is the 27th consecutive year that WBA or its predecessor company, Walgreen Co., has been named to the list. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">More company information is available at <U>www.walgreensbootsalliance.com</U>. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>WALGREENS BOOTS ALLIANCE, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>SUPPLEMENTAL INFORMATION (UNAUDITED) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>REGARDING <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> FINANCIAL MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(in millions, except per share amounts) </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
following information provides reconciliations of the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, as defined under SEC rules, presented in this press release to the most directly comparable financial measures
calculated and presented in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles in the United&nbsp;States&nbsp;(GAAP). The company has provided the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in the press release, which
are not calculated or presented in accordance with GAAP, as supplemental information and in addition to the financial measures that are calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">These supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are presented because management has evaluated the company&#146;s
financial results both including and excluding the adjusted items or the effects of foreign currency translation, as applicable, and believe that the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented provide
additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the company&#146;s business from period to period and trends in the company&#146;s historical operating results. These supplemental
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures should not be considered superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented in the press
release. The company does not provide a reconciliation for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> estimates on a forward-looking basis (including the information under &#147;Company Outlook&#148; above) where it is unable to provide a
meaningful or accurate calculation or estimation of reconciling items and the information is not available without unreasonable effort. This is due to the inherent difficulty of forecasting the timing or amount of various items that have not yet
occurred, are out of the company&#146;s control and/or cannot be reasonably predicted, and that would impact diluted net earnings per share, the most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure. For the same reasons, the company is
unable to address the probable significance of the unavailable information. Forward-looking <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provided without the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures may vary materially
from the corresponding GAAP financial measures. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Constant currency </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company also presents certain information related to current period operating results in &#147;constant currency,&#148; which is a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. These amounts are calculated by translating current period results at the foreign currency exchange rates used in the comparable period in the prior year. The company presents such
constant currency financial information because it has significant operations outside of the United States reporting in currencies other than the U.S. dollar and this presentation provides a framework to assess how its business performed excluding
the impact of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Comparable sales </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fiscal 2020 second-quarter comparable sales and prescriptions filled figures for the company&#146;s Retail Pharmacy divisions exclude the benefit of this
year&#146;s leap day. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the company&#146;s Retail Pharmacy divisions, comparable stores are defined as those that have been open for at least twelve
consecutive months without closure for seven or more consecutive days and without a major remodel or being subject to a natural disaster in the past twelve months. Relocated stores are not included as comparable stores for the first twelve months
after the relocation. Acquired stores are not included as comparable stores for the first twelve months after acquisition or conversion, when applicable, whichever is later. Comparable store sales, comparable pharmacy sales and comparable retail
sales refer to total sales, pharmacy sales and retail sales, respectively, in such stores. For the Retail Pharmacy USA division, comparable numbers of prescriptions refer to number of prescriptions in such stores. The method of calculating
comparable sales varies across the retail industry. As a result, the company&#146;s method of calculating comparable sales may not be the same as other retailers&#146; methods. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">With respect to the Retail Pharmacy International division, comparable store sales, comparable pharmacy
sales and comparable retail sales, are presented on a constant currency basis, which are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures. Refer to the discussion above in &#147;Constant currency&#148; for further details on
constant currency calculations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Key Performance Indicators </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company considers certain metrics, including all comparable metrics, number of prescriptions, number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT>
equivalent prescriptions and number of locations at period end, to be key performance indicators because the company&#146;s management has evaluated its results of operations using these metrics and believes that these key performance indicators
presented provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the company from period to period and trends in its historical operating results. These key performance indicators should not be considered
superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented herein. These measures may not be comparable to similarly-titled performance indicators used by other
companies. </P>
</DIV></Center>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Beginning in the quarter ended May&nbsp;31, 2019, management reviewed and refined its practice to reflect the
proportionate share of certain equity method investees&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items or unusual or infrequent items consistent with the company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures in order
to provide investors with a comparable view of performance across periods. These adjustments include acquisition-related amortization and acquisition-related costs and were immaterial for the prior periods presented. Although the company may have
shareholder rights and board representation commensurate with its ownership interests in these equity method investees, adjustments relating to equity method investments are not intended to imply that the company has direct control over their
operations and resulting revenue and expenses. Moreover, these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures have limitations in that they do not reflect all revenue and expenses of these equity method investees.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Free cash flow is defined as net cash provided by operating activities in a period less additions to property,
plant and equipment (capital expenditures) made in that period.&nbsp;This measure does not represent residual cash flows available for discretionary expenditures as the measure does not deduct the payments required for debt service and other
contractual obligations or payments for future business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flow as a measure that provides supplemental information to our entire statements of cash flows. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
